				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Ihr Menschen, rühmet Gottes Liebe, BWV 167 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1723 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Ihr Menschen, rühmet Gottes Liebe
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Ye mortals, extol God’s love
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ca">Ihr Menschen</span>; <span title="he">Ihr Menschen, rühmet Gottes Liebe, רי"ב 167</span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements:
<dl><dd>1. Aria (tenor): Ihr Menschen, rühmet Gottes Liebe
</dd><dd>2. Recitative (alto): Gelobet sei der Herr Gott Israel
</dd><dd>3. Duetto Aria (soprano): Gottes Wort, das trüget nicht
</dd><dd>4. Recitative (bass): Des Weibes Samen kam
</dd><dd>5. Chorale: Sei Lob und Preis mit Ehren
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
